  <span m='4325570'>Wei</span> <span m='4325890'>code,</span> <span m='4327460'>it</span>
  <span m='4327620'>gives</span> <span m='4327830'>you</span> <span m='4328060'>a</span>
  <span m='4328240'>very</span> <span m='4328580'>simple</span> <span m='4328970'>way</span>
  <span m='4329260'>to</span> <span m='4329430'>get</span> <span m='4329630'>4</span>
  <span m='4329860'>1/2</span> <span m='4330530'>dB.</span> <span m='4333750'>Actually,</span>
